shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_plan_A
	icon = GFX_GER_war_plan_A
	cost = 1
	prerequisite = {

	}
	allow_branch = {
		has_country_flag = GER_war_plan_A
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_plan_A"
		country_event = { id = goering.1003}
		set_variable = { scandinavia_nations_conquered = 1 }
		set_variable = { balkan_nations_conquered = 1 }

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = goering.50 days = 14
			}
			CRI = {
				set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
			}
			MOS = {
				set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
			}
			UKR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = UKR_koch
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = NOR_radicals
							has_global_flag = NOR_mainstream
							has_global_flag = NOR_moderates
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
				}
			}
			CAU = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = CAU_policy_business_goering
					}
					set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
				}
			}
			ROM = {
				set_country_flag = anti_goering_preparation
			}
			SWI = {

shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_the_german_bulldozer
	icon = GFX_GER_expand_frontier
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GGR_out_with_a_boom
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = GGR_a_call_for_help
	}
	available = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = PAU
				country_exists = TAM
				country_exists = DFK
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_the_german_bulldozer"


		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GGR_ignore_anti_goering_system
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.17 days = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = SMO }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SMO
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = PSK }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PSK
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = FRP }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FRP
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = RDC }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RDC
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = PAU }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PAU
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = PEN }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PEN
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MOS }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MOS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = OKB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OKB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = BBB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BBB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = RSB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RSB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ZLB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ZLB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_out_with_a_boom
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 2
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty < 30 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Influence > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Power > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_idea = GGR_last_legs
		}
	}
	x = -1
	y = 1
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_dont_question_your_orders
	icon = GFX_POL_germanys_loyal_sons
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GGR_the_german_bulldozer
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = OKB
	will_lead_to_war_with = PAU

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_dont_question_your_orders"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GGR_ignore_anti_goering_system
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.17 days = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				country_exists = OKB
				NOT = { has_war_with = OKB }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_dont_question_your_orders_tooltip
			declare_war_on = {
				target = OKB
				type = annex_everything
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					country_exists = PAU 
					NOT = { has_war_with = OKB }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PAU
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			add_war_support = -0.08
			add_stability = -0.06
			add_ideas = GGR_reluctant_soldiers
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				country_exists = PAU 
				NOT = { has_war_with = PAU }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PAU
				type = annex_everything
			}
			add_war_support = -0.08
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_dont_question_your_orders2_tooltip
			add_war_support = 0.08
		}
		clr_country_flag = GGR_operation_preparation
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_out_with_a_boom
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 2
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty < 50 }
		}
	}
	x = -1
	y = 2
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_a_call_for_help
	icon = GFX_ORE_accept_their_aid
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GGR_out_with_a_boom
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = GGR_the_german_bulldozer
	}
	available = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = PAU
			country_exists = TAM
			country_exists = DFK
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_a_call_for_help"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PAU
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PAU
				}
				MCW = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = DFK
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = DFK
				}
				MCW = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = TAM
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TAM
				}
				MCW = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		MCW = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = MCW_GER
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = PAU
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = PAU
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = DFK
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = DFK
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = TAM
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = TAM
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_socialism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_socialism
					popularity = 1
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Wolf-Heinrich Graf von Helldorff"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/Moskowien/PAU.dds"
					expire = "1999.10.12"
					ideology = national_socialism_subtype
					traits = { dictator }
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_military_supervision_no_supervision
					add_idea = tno_military_supervision_kill_em_all
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_racial_integration_integrated_military
					add_idea = tno_racial_integration_none
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MCW
					autonomous_state = autonomy_autonomous_reichskommissariat
				}
			}
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_out_with_a_boom
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 2
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty < 50 }
		}
	}
	x = 1
	y = 1
}

			}

shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_a_quick_war
	icon = GFX_GER_lightning_strike
	cost = 0.5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GGR_slovakian_remilitarization
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = HUN
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_a_quick_war"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = HUN
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GGR_operation_margarethe }
			HUN = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						is_puppet_of = ITA
					}
					ITA = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					load_oob = ITA_HUN_volunteers

				}
				ITA = { end_puppet = HUN }
				else = {
					set_global_flag = goring_invading_hun
					ITA = { end_puppet = HUN }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = GGR_operation_preparation
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_operation_margarethe
	x = 0
	y = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty < 30 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Influence > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Power > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_idea = GGR_last_legs
		}
	}
}

#Focus for Bombs Over Big Ben
shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_bombsoverbigben
	icon = GFX_generic_bombs
	relative_position_id = GGR_loadthetransports
	x = 3
	y = 1
	cost = 2
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	prerequisite = { focus = GGR_loadthetransports focus = GGR_radioblackout focus = GGR_fullsteamahead }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = ENG
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_bombsoverbigben"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ENG
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = GGR_keepthemblind }
			125 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = radar_station
					damage = 1
				}
			}
			126 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = radar_station
					damage = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GGR_wider_resistance }
				127 = {
					damage_building = {
						type = radar_station
						damage = 1
					}
				}
				123 = {
					damage_building = {
						type = radar_station
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GGR_radioblackout
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GGR_wider_resistance
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GGR_total_chaos
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			ENG_Kick_from_faction_balance = yes
			country_event = { id = ENG_sealion.101 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGR_wider_resistance
				has_completed_focus = GGR_radioblackout
			}
			ENG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GGR_total_chaos2
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GGR_operation_sealion2 }
		}
		clr_country_flag = GGR_operation_preparation
		clr_country_flag = GGR_wider_resistance
		clear_variable = GGR_naval_foci_done
		clear_variable = GGR_risks_taken
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty < 30 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Influence > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			check_variable = { GER_Militarist_Power > 75 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_idea = GGR_last_legs
		}
	}
}

			country_exists = FZL
			country_exists = ADL
			country_exists = TBA
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = IBR
	will_lead_to_war_with = SPR
	will_lead_to_war_with = SPS
	will_lead_to_war_with = FSR

	will_lead_to_war_with = TBA

			declare_war_on = {

			}
		}

		if = {

				country_exists = SPS
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SPS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FSR
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FSR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FZL
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FZL
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}

			}

					exists = yes
				}

					country_event = { id = goering.1218 days = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_central_russian_nation = yes
				}
				add_ideas = GGR_renewed_terror_bombing
				country_event = { id = goering.1216 days = 2 }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_central_russian_nation = yes
				}

			}
		}

						2 = {
							add_stability = -0.12
						}
						1 = {
							add_stability = 0.12
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = firebrands_manpower }
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_manpower = -8901
						}
						1 = {
							add_manpower = 8901
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = firebrands_factories }

						}

								type = infantry_equipment

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

				RWS = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			RWS = {

						}

							add_manpower = -8901
						}
						1 = {
							add_manpower = 8901
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = firebrands_factories }
					random_list = {
						1 = {
						}
						2 = {
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = infantry_equipment
								amount = 2500
								producer = GER
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GGR_hindered_war_effort
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GGR_hindered_war_effort
					add_idea = GGR_total_collapse
				}
			}
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_fall_rot

			}

	id = GER_GOR_it_is_their_turn_to_fear_the_dark
	icon = GFX_GER_it_is_their_turn_to_fear_the_dark
	cost = 2.00
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GGR_BRG_went_hot
		}
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GER_GOR_information_overload
		focus = GER_GOR_absolute_nuclear_coverage
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GER_GOR_it_is_their_turn_to_fear_the_dark"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					BRG_silent_war_spies = GER_silent_war_spies
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_1
				add_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_stalemate
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					BRG_silent_war_spies > GER_silent_war_spies
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_1
				add_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_lost
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					BRG_silent_war_spies < GER_silent_war_spies
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_1
				add_idea = GGR_the_silent_war_won
			}
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = GER_GOR_map_out_the_silos
	x = 0
	y = 2
}

		}

			econ_join_sphere_GER = yes

				hidden_effect = {

				econ_join_sphere_GER = yes
				leave_faction = yes
				GER = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_influence = 3 }
				}
				add_ideas = GGR_stalling_participation
				econ_join_sphere_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RKT = {
						owns_state = 627
						owns_state = 618
						owns_state = 617
						owns_state = 957
						owns_state = 958
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					transfer_state = 627

					transfer_state = 617
					transfer_state = 957
					transfer_state = 958
					add_state_core = 627
					add_state_core = 618
					add_state_core = 617
					add_state_core = 957
					add_state_core = 958
				}

shared_focus = {
	id = GGR_match_them
	icon = GFX_jap_break_from_navy
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GGR_challenge_the_USN_and_the_IJN
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: focus GGR_match_them "
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GGR_match_them
			days = 200
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = GGR_ship_count
			value = num_ships
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = GGR_USA_ship_count
			value = USA.num_ships
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = GGR_JAP_ship_count
			value = JAP.num_ships
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GGR_USA_ship_temp
			value = USA.num_ships
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GGR_USA_ship_temp
			value = 0.75
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GGR_JAP_ship_temp
			value = JAP.num_ships
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GGR_JAP_ship_temp
			value = 0.75
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = GGR_USA_ship_target
			value = GGR_USA_ship_temp
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = GGR_JAP_ship_target
			value = GGR_JAP_ship_temp
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GGR_USA_ship_target
					value = GGR_JAP_ship_target
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = GGR_ship_target
				value = GGR_JAP_ship_target
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GGR_USA_ship_target
					value = GGR_JAP_ship_target
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = GGR_ship_target
				value = GGR_USA_ship_target
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GGR_kriegsmarine_development
	}
	relative_position_id = GGR_challenge_the_USN_and_the_IJN
	x = -1
	y = 1
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_GOR_Militarwissenschaft
	icon = GFX_GER_wunderwaffe
	cost = 2

		focus = GER_GOR_lets_get_down_to_work
	}
	select_effect = {
		set_variable = { heer_centralisation = 0.3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = Picked_tank
			}
			add_to_variable = { heer_centralisation = 0.2 }
		}
		set_variable = { kriegsmarine_centralisation = 0.1 }
		set_country_flag = GGR_convincing_the_military
	}
	relative_position_id = GER_GOR_a_new_age_of_science
	x = 5
	y = 3
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_GOR_Militarwissenschaft"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_GOR_Militarwissenschaft_tooltip
		country_event = {
			id = goering.306
		}
		research_funding_maximal_increase_low = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { random_var = random }

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { random < heer_centralisation }
				}
				country_event = { id = goering.308 days = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = goering.307 days = 1 }
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { random < kriegsmarine_centralisation }
				}
				country_event = { id = goering.310 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = goering.309 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = GGR_convincing_the_military
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_GOR_das_liger
	icon = GFX_GER_das_liger
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GER_GOR_are_we_missing_something
	}
	relative_position_id = GER_GOR_a_new_age_of_science
	x = 7
	y = 9
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_GOR_das_liger"
		country_event = goering.320
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = goering.314 days = 4 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_remer_on_board
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_speidel_involved
				}
			}
			GGR_decrease_militarist_influence = yes
			clr_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_remer_on_board
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGRCSI_change_some_names
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_speidel_involved
				}
			}
			GGRCSI_decrease_military_power = yes
			clr_country_flag = GGRCSI_change_some_names
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_speidel_involved
			}
			GGR_decrease_militarist_influence_large = yes
			GGR_decrease_militarist_power_large = yes
			clr_country_flag = GGRCSI_get_speidel_involved
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_GOR_perfection
	icon = GFX_GER_aryan_generic
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GER_GOR_what_about_the_water
	}
	relative_position_id = GER_GOR_a_new_age_of_science
	x = -7
	y = 7
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_GOR_perfection"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGR_water_pacify_RK
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GGRCSI_perfection_pacify_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GGRCSI_perfection_water_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { loops = 0 }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { pipes_built > loops }
					}
					GGRCSI_decrease_military_power = yes
					add_to_temp_variable = { loops = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
